            $(function () {
                $('.helpbtn2').live('click', function (e) {
                    if (!$(this).data('helptext')) {
                        var p = $(this).parent(), c = 0;
                        while(!p.find('.helptext').length && c<5) {
                            p = p.parent();
                            c++;
                        }
                        if (!p.find('.helptext').length) {

                            $(this).remove();
                            return;
                        }
                        $(this).data('helptext', p.find('.helptext'));
                    }
                    if ($(this).data('helptext').is(":hidden")){
                        $(this).css({'padding-left': '10px', 'cursor':'pointer','color':'#a7a9ac'});
                    }else{
                        $(this).css({'padding-left': '10px', 'cursor':'pointer','color':'#00b0e8'});
                    }
                    $(this).data('helptext').slideToggle();
                });
            });

  <script type="text/javascript">
    //global vars
    window.cookieActiveLang = "RL_ACTIVE_LANG";

    function getCookie(cname){
        var name = cname + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++){
          var c = ca[i].trim();
          if (c.indexOf(name)==0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
        }
        return "";
    }
    function setCookie(cname,cvalue,exdays){
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime()+(exdays*24*60*60*1000));
        var expires = "expires="+d.toGMTString();
        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires;
    }

    //load common handlers
	$(function() {
		console.log('set cookie event handler ')

                //if ($(this).val() !== "russian" && $(this).val() !== "eigo") {
                
                if ($(this).val() !== "eigo") {
                    setCookie(cookieActiveLang, $(this).val(), 100);
                    
                }

    	    });
   
        
	})



//FIX FOR IE TRIM()
    if(typeof String.prototype.trim !== 'function') {
          String.prototype.trim = function() {
            return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''); 
          };
        }

</script>

        <div id="component-67086" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p><strong>Rocket Record allows you to listen to the way native speakers say hundreds of Spanish words and phrases. </strong>Then you can record yourself and accurately compare your speech with that of the native speaker.</p> 
          <p>It really is a fantastic way to learn Spanish by <strong>increasing the amount of Spanish vocabulary you know, and at the same time massively improving your Spanish pronunciation and accent.</strong> Rocket Record is great for your confidence!</p> 
          <p>Virtually every Spanish word and phrase in these lessons uses our Rocket Record voice comparison technology to <strong>get your pronunciation sounding as close as possible to a native South American.</strong></p>

         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67088" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p>Most of our Spanish lessons take advantage of the Testing section, which contains our exclusive testing tools. <strong>Testing has three testing components, Hear It Say It!, Write It!, and Know It! all scientifically designed to enhance your recall and understanding of spoken Spanish.</strong></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67089" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p class="h2">1. Hear it Say it!</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67090" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p><strong>Training your ear for Spanish can be one of the things that Spanish learners find the hardest to master. </strong>Thats why we came up with Hear It Say It!</p> 
          <p>Heres how Hear lt Say It! works. A randomly selected audio track from within each lesson is played. After listening to the track youre prompted to record yourself saying the word, compare the way you say it to the Spanish speaker, and rate how well you understand what the speaker was saying.<strong> A very powerful tool to tune your ear to spoken Spanish!</strong></p> 
          <p>Have a go with <em>Hear It Say It! </em>Here</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67091" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div ng-class="{'active-test': 'hearit' == activeTest }" class="panel rateable-test hearit" id="hearit"> 
          <div class="panel-heading"> 
           <div class="test-header"> 
            <div class="row row-fluid"> 
             <div class="col-xs-8 span8">

             </div> 
             <div class="col-xs-4 text-right panel-title span4"> 
              <div class="pull-right">

              </div>

        <div id="component-67092" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p class="h2">2. Write it!</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67093" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p>It's one thing being able to pronounce Spanish words correctly, it's quite another figuring out how those sounds turn into written words.</p> 
          <p>Write It! is the self-testing tool that lets you<strong> find out how well developed your Spanish ear really is. </strong>Just listen to the native speaker saying a word or phrase, then try to write it correctly in the space provided. There's a special character keyboard available if you need it, so you can get it exactly right.</p> 
          <p>When you're done click reveal, and you get to see how well you did, and get a rating for that word or phrase.</p> 
          <p>Test your writing skills with Write It! here:</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67094" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div ng-class="{'active-test': 'writeit' == activeTest }" class="panel rateable-test writeit" id="writeit"> 
          <div class="panel-heading"> 
           <div class="test-header"> 
            <div class="row row-fluid"> 
             <div class="col-xs-8 span8"> 
              <p class="h2 panel-title"> Write It! <a class="collapse-icon" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" data-target="#writeitInfo" aria-controls="collapseExample"> <i class="fa fa-info-circle info-trigger" style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 22px;"></i> </a> </p> 
             </div> 
             <div class="col-xs-4 text-right panel-title span4"> 
              <div class="pull-right"> 
               <a class="lesson-icon rateable rateable-icon level-<{ all.rateableTests['{{$rateableTest->name}}'].rating_level }>" uib-tooltip-html="'<strong>Write It!</strong><br /><{ all.rateableTests['writeit'].rating_label }>'" tooltip-placement="bottom" tooltip-append-to-body="true"> <i class="fa fa-pencil"></i> </a> 
              </div> 
              <span class="round-progress-percent-complete pull-right" ng-cloak> <span> <strong>&lt;{percentComplete['writeit']}&gt;%</strong> Complete </span> </span> 
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
           <div class="rateable-test-info collapsible collapse" id="writeitInfo"> 
            <p>Write it! helps you to improve your written Spanish and your understanding of sentence structures. Just listen to the audio and type in what you hear!</p> 
            <ul> 
             <li>Click the Get Started button below</li> 
             <li>LISTEN to the audio</li> 
             <li>WRITE down, in Spanish, what you hear</li> 
             <li>Click REVEAL to see the word/phrase and see the translation</li> 
             <li>Your answer will be automatically RATED, just click the rating to continue</li> 
            </ul> 
            <p><strong>Tip!</strong></p> 
            <p>Click the keyboard icon for a Spanish keyboard</p>

        <div id="component-67095" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p class="h2">3. Know it!</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67096" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div class="component text "> 
          <p>Now, all the training in the world wont help you<strong> if someone is talking to you in Spanish and your mind freezes when its your turn to speak!</strong> Thats why we developed Know It! The self-testing tool that really puts you on the spot!</p> 
          <p>Know It! pulls randomly selected English words and phrases out of each lesson and prompts you to record yourself saying the Spanish translation, compare yourself to the Spanish speaker, and then rate how well you did! You really need to know your stuff for this one but the benefits are huge in maximizing how quickly you can <strong>come up with the right thing to say when someone is speaking Spanish to you!</strong></p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div id="component-67099" class="component-wrapper"> 
         <div ng-class="{'active-test': 'knowit' == activeTest }" class="panel rateable-test knowit" id="knowit"> 
          <div class="panel-heading"> 
           <div class="test-header"> 
            <div class="row row-fluid"> 
             <div class="col-xs-8 span8"> 
              <p class="h2 panel-title"> Know It! <a class="collapse-icon" data-toggle="collapse" aria-expanded="true" data-target="#knowitInfo" aria-controls="collapseExample"> <i class="fa fa-info-circle info-trigger" style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 22px;"></i> </a> </p> 
             </div> 
             <div class="col-xs-4 text-right panel-title span4"> 
              <div class="pull-right"> 
               <a class="lesson-icon rateable rateable-icon level-<{ all.rateableTests['{{$rateableTest->name}}'].rating_level }>" uib-tooltip-html="'<strong>Know It!</strong><br /><{ all.rateableTests['knowit'].rating_label }>'" tooltip-placement="bottom" tooltip-append-to-body="true"> <i class="fa fa-lightbulb-o"></i> </a> 
              </div> 
              <span class="round-progress-percent-complete pull-right" ng-cloak> <span> <strong>&lt;{percentComplete['knowit']}&gt;%</strong> Complete </span> </span> 
             </div> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
           <div class="rateable-test-info collapsible collapse" id="knowitInfo"> 
            <p>Know it! tests you on your ability to translate English to Spanish! Ready?</p> 
            <ul> 
             <li>Click the Get Started button below</li> 
             <li>READ the word/phrase</li> 
             <li>RECORD yourself saying it in Spanish (Chrome/Firefox/Edge desktop browsers only)</li>

     <script type="text/javascript">


    var flyoutActive = false;


    function activeFlyoutCTA(viaEvent){
        $('.fly-out-cta.fly-out-cta-initial-state').addClass('fly-out-cta-active-state');
        console.log("Activating flyout via " + viaEvent);
        flyoutActive = true;
    }


    //Activate flyout after scrolling
    $(window).scroll (function() {
        if (($(window).scrollTop() > $(window).height()*0.5) && (flyoutActive == false))
        {      
            activeFlyoutCTA("scroll event");
        }
    })

    //Activate flyout after 5 seconds anyway
    setTimeout(function() {
        if (flyoutActive == false) {
            activeFlyoutCTA("time delay");
        }
    }, 5000);


    //Close flyout
    $( ".fly-out-cta-close" ).click(function() {     
        $('.fly-out-cta').removeClass('fly-out-cta-active-state fly-out-cta-initial-state').addClass('fly-out-cta-inactive-state');    
    });
    

</script> 
    </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
  $(document).ready(function(){



     
      

      $('.thePremium').hide();
      $('.thePlan').hide();      
      $('.theCombo').hide();      
      $('.theWorks').hide();


      var birdieUId = '';




      var affiliate = tid = '';
            
      var cookieLang = getCookie(cookieActiveLang);
      var urlLang = false;
      var selectedLang = window.selectedLang || ( urlLang || (cookieLang || 'spanish'));

//      console.log('urlLang',urlLang)
//      console.log('cookieLang',cookieLang)
//      console.log('selectedLang',selectedLang)




      





      for(var lang in product_data) {

        var option = product_data[lang].option;

        //override default selection
        
        if(selectedLang) option.selected = selectedLang == lang;


          
          $('.product-select').append($('<option value="'+lang+'" '+(option.selected ? 'selected="selected"' : '')+'>'+option.title+'</option>'));
        
        }
      
      $('.product-select').change(function() {

        var lang = $(this).val();

        affiliate = getCookie('aff['+lang+']') || getCookie('aff[global]') || affiliate;
        tid = getCookie('tid['+lang+']') || getCookie('tid[global]') || tid;
        //affiliate hop
        if( selectedLang != lang && //only hop when changing language
          typeof(affiliate) !== 'undefined' && affiliate) {
          window.location = "https://" + window.location.host + window.location.pathname + "?aff="+affiliate + "&tid="+tid + "&language="+lang + window.location.hash;
          return;
        }






        $('.noSurvivalKit').removeClass('noSurvivalKit');

        $('.notOnSignLanguages').show();
        $('.notOnEnglish').show();
        $('.thePremium').hide();
        $('.thePlan').hide();
        $('.theCombo').hide();
        $('.theWorks').hide();
        $('.freeBonus').show();
        $('.rocketPremiumPlus').hide();
        $('.rocketPlatinum').hide();
        $('.rocketPremiumPlusSurvival').hide();
        $('.rocketPlatinumSurvival').hide();
        $('.price-the-premium').find('p').html('<s>$149.95</s> <strong>$99.95</strong><br /><strong>+ $49.95 in bonus material FREE</strong>');

        IAL = 0;
        LC = 0;
        WL = 0;
        ASL = 0;
        VL = 0;
        voicePhrases = 0;


        $.each(product_data[lang]['products'],function(product, content){

            var current = product_data[lang]['premiumPageTextData'];
            packageNow = ''            

            if(lang!=="espanol"){ //hack for espanol which is otherwise called ingls
              $(".pricing-flag").attr("src", ("/images/flags/"+product_data[lang]['premiumPageTextData']['langLowerCase']+".png"));  
            } else {
              $(".pricing-flag").attr("src", ("/images/flags/espanol.png"));
            }            

            //PAYMENT OPTIONS
            $('.payment-options-link').attr("href", product_data[lang].paymentoptions);
            $('.payment-options-language').html(product_data[lang].premiumPageTextData.lang);



            
                  if (typeof product_data[lang].products.plus != "undefined") {
                    $('.order-the-plus, .premium-plus-sales-link a').attr("href", product_data[lang].products.plus.orderpage.download);

                  }

                  if (typeof product_data[lang].products.plat != "undefined") {
                    $('.order-the-platinum, .platinum-sales-link a').attr("href", product_data[lang].products.plat.orderpage.download);
                  }

             

            if (typeof product_data[lang].packages.thePremium != "undefined") {
              $('.order-the-premium-shipped, .order-the-premium-shipped').attr("href", product_data[lang].packages.thePremium.orderLinkShipped);
            }

            if (typeof product_data[lang].packages.theCombo != "undefined") {
              $('.order-the-combo-shipped, .order-the-combo-shipped').attr("href", product_data[lang].packages.theCombo.orderLinkShipped);
            }

            if (typeof product_data[lang].packages.theWorks != "undefined") {
              $('.order-the-works-shipped, .order-the-works-shipped').attr("href", product_data[lang].packages.theWorks.orderLinkShipped);
            }
            
            if(product=='prem'){
                packageNow = 'thePremium';
                $('.rocketPremiumText').html(content['name']);
                $('.rocketPremiumSurvivalText').html(content['survivalKit']);
                $('.speakLevel').html(product_data[lang]['premiumPageTextData']['lang']);

            }
            else if(product=='plus'){
                packageNow = 'theCombo';
                $('.rocketPremiumPlus').show();
                $('.rocketPremiumPlusText').html(content['name']);
                $('.rocketPremiumPlusSurvival').show();
                $('.rocketPremiumPlusSurvivalText').html(content['survivalKit']);

            }

            else if(product=='plat'){
                packageNow = 'theWorks';
                  
                $('.rocketPlatinum').show();
                $('.rocketPlatinumText').html(content['name']);
                $('.rocketPlatinumSurvival').show();
                $('.rocketPlatinumSurvivalText').html(content['survivalKit']);
            }

            else if(product=='freetrial'){
              packageNow = 'freeTrial';
            }

       


            if(product!=='freetrial'){
              
            var currentPackage = product_data[lang]['packages'][packageNow];
            $('.'+packageNow)      

                              .find('.orderLink').attr('href',currentPackage['orderLink']).end()
                           
             
                            
              .find('.orderLinkPlan').attr('href',currentPackage['orderLinkPlan']).end()
              .find('.orderLinkShipped').attr('href',currentPackage['orderLinkShipped']).end()

              .find('.price')
                .filter('.original').text(currentPackage['prices']['original']).end()
                .filter('.shipped').text(currentPackage['prices']['shipped']).end()
                .filter('.plan').text(currentPackage['prices']['plan']).end()
                .filter('.plan-current').text(currentPackage['prices']['plan-current']).end()
                .filter('.current').text(currentPackage['prices']['current']).end()
                .filter('.saving').text(currentPackage['prices']['saving']).end()
                .filter('.plan-saving').text(currentPackage['prices']['plan-saving']).end()                
                .filter('.bonus').each(function() {
                  //hide the bonus div if no bonus
                  if(currentPackage['prices']['bonus'] == "") {
                    $(this).parents('.bonusText').hide();
                  } else {
                    $(this).text(currentPackage['prices']['bonus']).end();
                  }
                }).end()

                
              .end()
              .show()
            

            IAL += parseInt(content['IAL']||0);
            LC += parseInt(content['LC']||0);
            WL += parseInt(content['WL']||0);
            ASL += parseInt(content['ASL']||0);
            VL += parseInt(content['VL']||0);
            voicePhrases += parseInt(content['voicePhrases']|| 0);

            $('.onSignLanguages').hide();
            $('.onEnglish').hide();
            $('.cd-set').hide();
            $('.thePlan').hide();
            $('.colspan').attr('colspan',1);            
            $('.level-1-title').show();
            $('.single-level-language').hide();  
            $('.multi-level-language').hide();  
            
            $('table.pricing-table .thePremium:not(.transparent-background), table.pricing-table .theWorks:not(.transparent-background), table.pricing-table .theCombo:not(.transparent-background), .pricing-option.thePremium, .pricing-option.theWorks:not(.transparent-background), .pricing-option.theCombo:not(.transparent-background)').css("background-color","#d5e7f6");
           
            $('.option').show();

            //---special cases
            if(lang=='sign-language'){
                $('.cdset').show();
                $('.onSignLanguages').show();
                $('.notOnSignLanguages').hide();
                $('.order.thePremium, .price.current').addClass('noSurvivalKit');
            }

            if(lang=='english'){
                $('.notOnEnglish').hide();
                $('.onEnglish').show();
                $('.order.thePremium, .price.current').addClass('noSurvivalKit');
            }

            if(lang=='english' || lang=='espanol' || lang=='eigo' || lang=='sign-language'){
                $('.freeBonus').hide();
            }

            $('.haveWritingLesson').hide();
            if(lang=='chinese' || lang=='japanese' || lang=='hindi' || lang=='korean' || lang=='arabic' || lang=='russian'){
                $('.haveWritingLesson').show();
            }

            if(lang=='portuguese' || lang=='korean' || lang=='hindi' || lang=='arabic' || lang=='russian' || lang=='english' || lang=='sign-language'
                
                 

              )
            {

                $('.thePremium:not(.thePlan, .cd-set, .transparent-background)').css("background-color","#acc6dd");         
                
                $('.single-level-language').show();            


                $('.thePlan').show();

                
                if(lang!='english' && lang!='sign-language' && lang!='russian' && lang!='espanol'){

                  $('.cd-set').show();
                  $('.colspan').attr('colspan',2);
                
                } else {

                  $('.option').hide();
                  $('.colspan').attr('colspan',1);                  
                }

            } else { 

                $('.multi-level-language').show();
                $("table .theWorks:not(.transparent-background)").css("background-color","#acc6dd");

            }

            

            //---END special cases
            
            $('.'+packageNow)
              .find('.IAL').html(IAL).end()
              .find('.LC').html(LC).end()
              .find('.WL').html(WL).end()
              .find('.ASL').html(ASL).end()
              .find('.VL').html(VL).end()
              .find('.flashcards').html(IAL+LC).end()
              .find('.lessonTotal').html(IAL+LC+ASL+VL+WL).end()
              .find('.lessonHours').html(2*(IAL+LC+ASL+VL)).end()
              .find('.voicePhrases').html(voicePhrases).end()

            }

            $.each($('.feature-details'), function() {
                $(this).attr({'data-original-title': $(this).closest('td').find('.feature-details-copy').text()})
            });

        });

        //if the promo exists, reload it for this language
        if(window.promo) {
          // console.log('loadFrontendPromo',lang);
          loadFrontendPromo(lang);
        }

                   
           
            //update prices for new coupon system
            var orderpageCoupon = 'ROCKETDEAL';
            if (orderpageCoupon.length > 0){
              $(".orderLink, .orderLinkPlan").each(function(){          
                $(this).attr("href", $(this).attr("href") + "?coupon=" + orderpageCoupon);         
              });
            }

          
        

      
      });      

      $('.product-select').change();

  });
</script>

    <div class="span9"> 
     <h3>Who am I?</h3> 
     <p> <strong> Hola, my names Mauricio, and Im the host of Rocket Spanish. </strong> I come from the beautiful country of Chile, which means Latin American Spanish is my native language. That also means that I know just how hard it can be to learn a new language, because Ive been there learning English. Together with my English speaking colleague, Amy, I want to help you to speak and understand Spanish while cutting your learning time in half. </p> 
     <p> Ive travelled the world over and have found that languages are a great way to meet people and discover new things. I really want to make your Spanish learning experience rewarding and fun! </p> 
     <p style="padding:0; margin:0">My goal, just like Rocket Languages, is to help you reach your goal.</p>

  <script type="text/javascript">


$(document).ready (function() {  

  //expanded short privacy policy
  $(".extend-privacy-policy").live( "click", function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    $(".privacy-policy").toggle();
    $(".extended-privacy-policy").toggle();
  });  

  window.selectedLang = "spanish"

  $('.free-trial-form').load("../../../includes/trial-signup/main-arpreach.php?homepage&language="+selectedLang, {lang:selectedLang,adtrack:'homepage'});
  $('.tutor').html(product_data[selectedLang]['premiumPageTextData']['tutor1']); 



  //changing the page copy and examples  
  console.log('loading trial selector')

  
  $('.product-select').live('change', function(){
    
    console.log('change trial select');
    

    if($(this).val() == "ingles") {
      window.selectedLang = "espanol";
    } else {
      window.selectedLang = $(this).val();
    } 
       
    $('img.trial-flag').attr("src", '/images/flags/'+selectedLang+'.png');
    $('.tutor').html(product_data[selectedLang]['premiumPageTextData']['tutor1']);     
    $('.learn-more').attr("href", selectedLang+"/premium");
    $('.buylink').attr("href", selectedLang+"/rocket-"+selectedLang+"-premium.php#courses-and-pricing");  
    $('.language').html(selectedLang.replace("-"," "));

    
    $('.copy-english').hide(); 
    $('.copy-eigo').hide(); 
    $('.copy-ingles').hide(); 
    
    if (($(this).val() !== 'eigo') && ($(this).val() !== 'espanol')){
      $('.copy-english').show();
      $('input#guestAccess').val("Get Instant Access to your Guest User trial");    
    } else {      
      if ($(this).val() == 'eigo') {
        $('.buylink').attr("href", "https://order.rocketlanguages.com/eigo-premium");      
        $('.copy-eigo').show(); 
        $('input#guestAccess').val("????????????????????????");
      } 
      if ($(this).val() == 'espanol') {
        $('.buylink').attr("href", "https://order.rocketlanguages.com/ingles-premium");  
        $('.copy-ingles').show(); 
        $('input#guestAccess').val("Obtenga acceso a su Perodo de Prueba como Usuario Invitado");
      } 
    }


    if ($(this).val() == 'sign-language') {
      $('.language').html(selectedLang.replace("-"," "));
      $('.hidden-sign-language').hide(); 
    } else {
      $('.hidden-sign-language').show();
    }

    if ($(this).val() == 'english') {
      $('.hidden-english').hide();
      $('.buylink').attr("href", "https://www.rocketlanguages.com/english/premium/general.php#courses-and-pricing");
    } else {
      $('.hidden-english').show();
    }





    //updating the free trial form
    $('.free-trial-form').load("../../../includes/trial-signup/main-arpreach.php?homepage&language="+selectedLang, {lang:selectedLang,adtrack:'homepage','referrer': "www.rocketlanguages.com/spanish/learn/learn-spanish-online "});
    

  }).change(); // ./product-select

  //sign up to guest access (no password or email requred account) 
  $("#guestAccess").click(function() {

      $(".guest-loading").show();

      window.location = '/guest/'+selectedLang+'/activate/go';
      window.location.href = '/guest/'+selectedLang+'/activate/go';
  }) // ./click
})

</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
$(function () {
  <!-- accordion script -->
  $('#navig').find('a').click(function (e) {
    if ($(this).attr('href') == '#') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if ($(this).parent().children('ul').length) {
            if ($(this).parent().children('ul').filter(':visible').length) {
                $(this).parent().children('ul').slideUp();
            }else{
                $(this).parent().children('ul').slideDown();
            }
        }
    }
  });
  $('.dropdown-linked a').on('click', function () {
     if ($(this).attr('href').substr(0, 1) == '#') {
        var item = $($(this).attr('href'));
        if (item.length) {
            if (!item.hasClass('current')) {
              console.log(item,item.parent().children('ul'))
                item.parents('ul').find('ul').hide();
                item.click();
            }
        }
     }
  })
});
// $('#navig').find('ul ul').hide();
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    //global vars
    window.cookieActiveLang = "RL_ACTIVE_LANG";

    function getCookie(cname){
        var name = cname + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++){
          var c = ca[i].trim();
          if (c.indexOf(name)==0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
        }
        return "";
    }
    function setCookie(cname,cvalue,exdays){
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime()+(exdays*24*60*60*1000));
        var expires = "expires="+d.toGMTString();
        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires;
    }

    //load common handlers
	$(function() {
		console.log('set cookie event handler ')

    		$('.product-select').live('change',function() {
                
                //if ($(this).val() !== "russian" && $(this).val() !== "eigo") {
                
                if ($(this).val() !== "eigo") {
                    setCookie(cookieActiveLang, $(this).val(), 100);
                    
                }

    	    });
   
        
	})



//FIX FOR IE TRIM()
    if(typeof String.prototype.trim !== 'function') {
          String.prototype.trim = function() {
            return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g, ''); 
          };
        }

</script>

    $(document).ready(function(){
    var now = new Date();
    var today = new String;
    var m = ['January','February','March','April','May','June','July',
        'August','September','October','November','December'];
    today = m[now.getMonth()] + ' ' + now.getDate() + ', ' + now.getFullYear();

  <script type="text/javascript">

//TRIGGER POPUP
$( ".trigger-trialsignup-call-fullpage" ).click(function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    $("body").css({'height':'100%', 'overflow' : 'hidden'});
    $(".full-page-exit-popup-wrapper").css({'display':'table'});
});

//HIDE EXIT POPUP
$( ".full-page-exit-popup-close" ).live( "click", function(event) {
  event.preventDefault();
  $('body').css({'overflow' : 'inherit'});
  $('.full-page-exit-popup-wrapper').hide();
}); 


$(function(){
  $('#arp-subscription-form')
  .submit(function(e){
    e.preventDefault();

      var me = $(this);
      $(this).find('input.submit').css('display','none');
      $(this).find('img.loader').css('display','block');

        try { 
          ga('send', 'pageview', '/newslettersignup/');
fbq('track', 'Lead');
          ga('send', 'event', 'NewsletterSignup', '', "\/spanish\/learn\/learn-spanish-online");
        
        } catch(err) {}

        //post the actual data
        $.post("/includes/trial-signup/main-arpreach.php",
        {
          name:$(this).find('input[name=name]').val(),
          email:$(this).find('input[name=email]').val().replace(/\s+/g, ''),
          confirm_email:$(this).find('input[name=confirm_email]').val(),
          adtrack: "",
          inc: null,
          lang:"spanish",
          referrer:window.location.href,
          submitted:true
        },function(r) {

        $(".temperror").hide().html("");

        if (r.errors.email){
          $(".temperror.email-error").show().html(r.errors.email);
        }

        if (r.errors.name){
          $(".temperror.name-error").show().html(r.errors.name);
        }

        //update ui
        $('.error-msg').text('');

        if(!r.success && r.msg) {
          me.find('input.submit').css('display','block');
          me.find('img.loader').css('display','none');
          //$('.error-msg').show();
          $('.error-msg').text(r.msg);
          $(".form-input-titles").show();
        }
        if(r.success && r.hash && r.redirect) {
          // console.log(me.submit)
          window.location = r.redirect;
        }
      },'json');
    return false;
  });
});
</script>
